hideParentAndResetTrigger=function(){hideParent();sloppyTrigger.disable();};for(var i=0;i<linkKeys.length;i++){var item=linkKeys[i];if(item.panelKey){addPanel(item.link,item.panelKey);}else{item.link.mouseover(hideParentAndResetTrigger);}}};});
      } catch ( err ) {
        if ( window.$Nav ) {
          window.$Nav.when('metrics', 'logUeError').run(function(metrics, log) {
            metrics.increment('NavJS:AboveNavInjection:error');
            log(err.toString(), {
              'attribution': 'rcx-nav',
              'logLevel': 'FATAL'
            });
          });
        }
      }
    </script>
